How familiar are you with GLP-1s?
GLP-1 is a natural hormone that makes you feel full and helps control your blood sugar.

These medications work similarly to help you lose weight by:
  • Slowing down how food moves through your stomach and intestines.
  • Making you feel full for longer.
  • Helping your body use insulin better.
